interconnected subsystems:\\n\\n## Cluster Discovery Service (CDS)\\n\\nThe CDS implementation is centered in `source/common/upstream/` where:\\n- `cds_api_impl.cc/h` implements the core CDS subscription mechanism, extending `Envoy::Config::SubscriptionBase<envoy::config::cluster::v3::Cluster>` and managing cluster discovery requests through gRPC\\n- `cds_api_helper.cc/h` provides a helper class that handles configuration updates from the subscription, processing added and removed clusters\\n- `od_cds_api_impl.cc/h` implements On-Demand CDS (ODCDS) for dynamic cluster discovery on-demand, supporting lazy cluster loading\\n- `cluster_discovery_manager.cc/h` manages the overall cluster discovery workflow\\n\\n## Cluster Manager Integration\\n\\nThe cluster manager coordinates cluster lifecycle and updates:\\n- `cluster_manager_impl.cc/h` is the central cluster management implementation that orchestrates CDS subscriptions, creates and manages cluster instances, handles cluster initialization, and manages thread-local updates\\n- `cluster_factory_impl.cc/h` creates cluster instances with proper health checkers and load balancers configured\\n- `cluster_update_tracker.cc/h` tracks cluster updates via callbacks from the cluster manager\\n\\n## Active Health Checking\\n\\nHealth checking is implemented across multiple layers:\\n\\n**Core Health Checker Framework:**\\n- `health_checker_impl.cc/h` provides the base active health checker implementation, managing health check sessions and scheduling\\n- `health_checker_event_logger.cc/h` logs health checking events for debugging and observability\\n- `health_discovery_service.cc/h` implements the gRPC health discovery service for remote health status reporting\\n\\n**Health Checker Extensions:**\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.cc/h` provides the base implementation for all health checker types\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/http/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements HTTP health checking with request/response validation\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/tcp/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements TCP health checking with connection validation\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.cc/h` implements gRPC health checking using the standard gRPC health check protocol\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/redis/redis.cc/h` implements Redis-specific health checking\\n- `source/extensions/health_checkers/thrift/thrift.cc/h` implements Thrift health checking\\n\\n**Health Checker Integration:**\\n- `upstream_impl.cc/h` contains the `ClusterImplBase::setHealthChecker()` method that integrates health checkers with cluster instances\\n\\n## Outlier Detection Integration\\n\\n- `outlier_detection_impl.cc/h` implements outlier detection that tracks host health and ejects unhealthy hosts based on configured detection algorithms\\n- Outlier detection integrates with the health checking system to mark hosts as ejected when thresholds are exceeded\\n\\n## gRPC/XDS Configuration Subscription\\n\\nCDS is delivered through gRPC subscriptions implemented in `source/extensions/config_subscription/grpc/`:\\n\\n**Subscription Management:**\\n- `grpc_subscription_impl.cc/h` provides the gRPC subscription implementation for any resource type\\n- `grpc_subscription_factory.cc/h` creates subscription instances for different resource types\\n\\n**gRPC Mux Implementation (Legacy):**\\n- `grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` implements the original gRPC multiplexer for aggregated discovery service (ADS)\\n- `new_grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` provides an improved implementation with better resource caching and management\\n\\n**XDS Mux (Modern Implementation):**\\n- `xds_mux/grpc_mux_impl.cc/h` implements the XDS protocol mux for handling multiple resource types\\n- `xds_mux/sotw_subscription_state.cc/h` manages State-of-the-World (SotW) subscription state\\n- `xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc/h` manages Delta subscription state for incremental updates\\n- `xds_mux/subscription_state.h` defines the subscription state interface\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.cc/h` handles aggregated collection subscriptions\\n- `watch_map.cc/h` manages watches for different resource types\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.cc/h` implements acknowledgment queue management with pause/resume capability\\n- `delta_subscription_state.cc/h` and related files handle delta subscription state\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h` caches Endpoint Discovery Service (EDS) resources for efficient memory usage\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h` provides context for gRPC mux implementations\\n- `grpc_stream.h` and `grpc_stream_interface.h` define the streaming protocol\\n- `xds_source_id.cc/h` manages XDS source identifiers\\n- `update_ack.h` defines acknowledgment structures\\n\\n## Load Stats Reporting\\n\\n- `load_stats_reporter.cc/h` implements reporting of load and resource statistics back to the control plane through the Load Reporting Service (LRS)\\n\\nThese files collectively implement Envoy's dynamic cluster discovery through CDS subscriptions, active health checking of cluster endpoints with multiple protocol support (HTTP, gRPC, TCP, Redis, Thrift), outlier detection integration for automatic host ejection, and the complete gRPC/XDS control plane communication infrastructure.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":817,"cache_read_input_tokens":74489,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":817},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"28c3b876-969a-4719-b699-3ea1d53e8317","uuid":"2baaaa47-4954-4d74-813a-7f633fe2f637"}

subscription state\\n- `xds_mux/delta_subscription_state.cc/h` manages Delta subscription state for incremental updates\\n- `xds_mux/subscription_state.h` defines the subscription state interface\\n\\n**Supporting Infrastructure:**\\n- `grpc_collection_subscription_factory.cc/h` handles aggregated collection subscriptions\\n- `watch_map.cc/h` manages watches for different resource types\\n- `pausable_ack_queue.cc/h` implements acknowledgment queue management with pause/resume capability\\n- `delta_subscription_state.cc/h` and related files handle delta subscription state\\n- `eds_resources_cache_impl.cc/h` caches Endpoint Discovery Service (EDS) resources for efficient memory usage\\n- `grpc_mux_context.h` provides context for gRPC mux implementations\\n- `grpc_stream.h` and `grpc_stream_interface.h` define the streaming protocol\\n- `xds_source_id.cc/h` manages XDS source identifiers\\n- `update_ack.h` defines acknowledgment structures\\n\\n## Load Stats
